   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of lunar probes
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>

         </div>

      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:277px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1270" data-file-width="1459" height="239" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg/275px-Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg/413px-Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg/550px-Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg 2x" width="275"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Surveyor_3_on_Moon.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Surveyor_3" title="Surveyor 3">
          Surveyor 3
         </a>
         on the Moon.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Luna_3_moon.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="384" data-file-width="500" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Luna_3_moon.jpg/220px-Luna_3_moon.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Luna_3_moon.jpg/330px-Luna_3_moon.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Luna_3_moon.jpg/440px-Luna_3_moon.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Luna_3_moon.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The first image returned by
         <i>
          Luna 3
         </i>
         showed the far side of the Moon
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       This is a list of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_probes" title="Space probes">
        space probes
       </a>
       that have flown by, impacted, or landed on the
       <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">
        Moon
       </a>
       for the purpose of
       <a href="/wiki/Exploration_of_the_Moon" title="Exploration of the Moon">
        lunar exploration
       </a>
       , as well as probes launched toward the Moon that failed to reach their target. Confirmed future probes are included, but missions that are still at the concept stage, or which never progressed beyond the concept stage, are not.
      </p>
      <p>
       The list does not include the manned
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Project_Apollo" title="Project Apollo">
        Apollo
       </a>
       missions.
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Key">
        Key
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_lunar_probes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Key">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Colour key:
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <table>
         <tr>
          <td>
           <span style="background-color:#EFE7B8;; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">
           </span>
           – Mission or flyby completed successfully (or partially successfully)
          </td>
          <td>
          </td>
          <td>
           <span style="background-color:#F2F2F2;; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">
           </span>
           – Failed or cancelled mission
          </td>
         </tr>
         <tr>
          <td>
           <span style="background-color:#CCFFD9;; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">
           </span>
           – Mission en route or in progress (including mission extensions)
          </td>
          <td>
          </td>
          <td>
           <span style="background-color:#FFFFFF;; color:black; border:1px solid darkgray; text-align:center;">
           </span>
           – Planned mission
          </td>
          <td>
          </td>
         </tr>
        </table>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <sup>
         †
        </sup>
        means "tentatively identified", as classified by NASA
        <a class="external autonumber" href="http://nssdc.gsfc.nasa.gov/planetary/tent_launch.html" rel="nofollow">
         [1]
        </a>
        . These are Cold War-era Soviet missions, mostly failures, about which few or no details have been officially released. The information given may be speculative.
        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
         [
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Precise_language" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">
           <span title="The text near this tag is dated.">
            needs update
           </span>
          </a>
         </i>
         ]
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Date
        </b>
        is the date of:
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li>
          closest encounter (flybys)
         </li>
         <li>
          impact (impactors)
         </li>
         <li>
          orbital insertion to end of mission, whether planned or premature (orbiters)
         </li>
         <li>
          landing to end of mission, whether planned or premature (landers)
         </li>
         <li>
          launch (missions that never got underway due to failure at or soon after launch)
         </li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        In cases which do not fit any of the above, the event to which the date refers is stated. Note that as a result of this scheme missions are
        <i>
         not
        </i>
        always listed in order of launch.
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <ul>
       <li>
        In the case of flybys (such as gravity assists) that are incidental to the main mission, "success" indicates the successful completion of the flyby, not necessarily that of the main mission.
       </li>
      </ul>

         </i>
        </td>
        <td>
         <span class="flagicon">
          <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
           <img alt="United States" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
          </a>
         </span>
         <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">
          DOD
         </a>
        </td>
        <td>
         17 August 1958
        </td>
        <td>
         orbiter
        </td>
        <td>
         failure
        </td>
        <td>
         first attempted launch beyond Earth orbit; launch vehicle failure; maximum altitude 16 km
        </td>
        <td>
         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pioneer_able.png">
          <img alt="Pioneer able.png" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="586" height="43" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Pioneer_able.png/50px-Pioneer_able.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Pioneer_able.png/75px-Pioneer_able.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Pioneer_able.png/100px-Pioneer_able.png 2x" width="50"/>
         </a>
        </td>
        <td>
         <a class="external autonumber" href="http://nssdc.gsfc.nasa.gov/nmc/spacecraftDisplay.do?id=ABLE1" rel="nofollow">
          [2]
         </a>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="background:#F2F2F2">
        <td colspan="2">
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Luna_E-1_No.1" title="Luna E-1 No.1">
           Luna E-1 No.1
          </a>
         </i>
        </td>
        <td>
